# Pan Flute

# Description __

A set of repurposed PVC pipes that can be used to play a variety of melodies.

Page views: 3,522  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Acoustic Guitar

# Description __

A classic acoustic guitar, built for jam sessions around campfires at night.

Page views: 4,334  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Jerry Can Guitar

# Description __

Take advantage of the unique acoustics of the Jerry Can Guitar to play some rustic tunes.

Page views: 4,214  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Canbourine

# Description __

A selection of crumpled cans assembled into a ring to produce some great background percussion.

Page views: 3,522  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Sousaphone

# Description __

A collection of used piping that’s been converted into a Tuba. Probably not very hygienic.

Page views: 3,145  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Furnace

# Description __

A Furnace. Use it to smelt mined ore.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x200 Stone
  * x100 Wood
  * x50 Low Grade Fuel



## Recycling Output __

  * x100 Stone
  * x500 Wood
  * x25 Low Grade Fuel



# Usage __

The furnace smelts one item from each stack at the same time.

Page views: 5,349  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/furnace.large~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/furnace.large~history)



# Large Furnace

# Description __

Used to smelt large quantities of ore. Difficult to secure, must be placed on terrain.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x500 Stone
  * x600 Wood
  * x75 Low Grade Fuel



## Recycling Output __

  * x250 Stone
  * x300 Wood
  * x38 Low Grade Fuel



Page views: 4,482  
Updated: This Year

# Electric Fuse

# Description __

An unreliable electric fuse. Will allow electrical passthrough for a period of time.

Page views: 5,549  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# High External Stone Gate

# Description __

A high stone gate, allowing access in and out of your compound.

# High External Wooden Gate

# Description __

A high wooden gate, allowing access in and out of your compound.

Page views: 4,060  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Geiger Counter

# Description __

A geiger counter used by scientists.

This item is not obtainable in vanilla Rust.

Page views: 5,405  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Wind Turbine

# Description __

Converts kinetic energy harvested from the wind into electricity. Amount generated will vary depending on wind speed. Higher altutides will yield stronger winds.

Page views: 8,182  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Glue

# Description __

A strong adhesive.

This item is not obtainable in vanilla rust.

Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Granola Bar

# Description __

Granola Bar found as loot. Eating it provides a small boost to health, hunger.

Page views: 4,668  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/grenade.beancan~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/grenade.beancan~history)



# Beancan Grenade

# Description __

_Unreliable explosive grenade._   
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  


# Infomation __

The Beancan Grenade is an early-game tool. They're used to craft Satchel Charges, but can be used by themselves in raiding. The Beancan Grenade has a random detonation period and can kill a player if it's within the range. The Beancan Grenade has a 15% chance to be a dud. However, Beancan Grenades have a 50% chance to explode when you attempt to pick them up again after a dud.

# Stats __

  * Explosive Dmg: **15**
  * Lethality: **115**
  * Throw Distance: **26m**
  * Fuse Length: **3.5-4s**
  * Blast Radius: **4.5m**



# Researching __

  * **715x** [Scrap](scrap) to go thru the tech tree in a [Work Bench Level 1](workbench1)
  * **75x** [Scrap](scrap) at the [Research Table](research.table)



# Crafting __

  * **60x** [Gun Powder](gunpowder)
  * **20x** [Metal Fragments](metal.fragments)



# Recycle __

  * **30x** [Gun Powder](gunpowder)
  * **10x** [Metal Fragments](metal.fragments)



# Repair __

Can't be Repaired

# Loot __

  * **2%** Elite Tier Crate
  * **2%** Heavy Scientist
  * **2%** Underwater Lab Elite Crate
  * **1%** Sunken Chest
  * **1%** Underwater Lab Blue Crate
  * **1%** Crate
  * **0.2%** Arctic Scientist
  * **0.2%** Tunnel Dweller
  * **0.2%** Cargo Ship Scientist
  * **0.2%** Underwater Dweller
  * **0.2%** Military Base Scientist
  * **0.2%** Excavator Scientist
  * **0.2%** Oil Rig Scientist
  * **0.2%** Patrol Scientist

# F1 Grenade

# Description __

Reliable explosive grenade. Deals little structural damage but is devastating to enemy players with a well-placed throw.

Page views: 9,069  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Smoke Grenade

# Description __

Produces a large cloud of opaque greyish white smoke.

Page views: 5,624  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Gun Powder

# Description __

Made from Sulfur and Charcoal, a key ingredient of anything that goes bang!

Page views: 4,264  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Shotgun Trap

# Description __

A shotgun trap triggered by movement, place near doorways and load with handmade shells.

Page views: 9,397  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Halloween Candy

# Description __

Some loose halloween candy Collect 10 to upgrade to a Small Loot Bat!

Page views: 3,073  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Medium Loot Bag

# Description __

Contains medium level loot, Collect 10 to upgrade to a Large loot bag, containing the best loot

Page views: 3,952  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Small Loot Bag

# Description __

Open for a surprise, or collect 10 to upgrade to a medium loot bag containing better loot!
